[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run using Jazzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibFuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on a CSV parsing target timed out after [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproximately [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m seconds. The main thread is stuck in native callbacks invoked by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe data-flow tracing instrumentation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while processing CSV [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput via Apache Tika’s `TextAndCSVParser`. No crash or exception is reported—only [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma sustained hang leading to a timeout.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzing session terminated with an `ERROR: libFuzzer: timeout` message. The [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJVM thread dump shows the “main” thread in a RUNNABLE state, executing the native [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod `TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceConstCmpInt`, which is part of the Jazzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation. The stack trace leads into Apache Tika’s CSV parsing logic, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically through `CellFormatter.format` and `TextAndCSVParser.parse`, and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfinally into the user-provided harness methods `parseOne` and `fuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While no memory corruption or exception is observed, the symptom is a hang or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfinite loop—effectively a denial-of-service condition if triggered in production.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is often classified as a “hang” or “timeout” vulnerability under availability [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missues.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The hang occurs repeatedly at the same native callback point [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The CSV parser entry points involved are `CellFormatter.format` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser.parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m200[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness calls `TextAndCSVParserFuzzer.parseOne` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m57[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m then [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m41[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The issue does not manifest as a crash, but the execution does not complete [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the allotted libFuzzer timeout.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Apache Tika CSV Parsing Logic**  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Review `TextAndCSVParser.parse` to identify loops or state machines that [0m    [2m                [0m
